# Prune edges from a modality graph

Removes weak or non-significant edges from a `catmodgraph` object. This
is the modality-level analogue of
[`prune_edges()`](https://atinakosta.github.io/catgraph/reference/prune_edges.md)
for variable graphs.

## Usage

``` r
prune_modality_edges(x, min_weight = 0, max_p = 1, remove_isolates = FALSE)
```

## Arguments

- x:

  A `catmodgraph` object.

- min_weight:

  Numeric, non-negative. Edges with phi strictly below this value are
  removed. Since phi lies in \[0, 1\], meaningful thresholds are usually
  in that range. Default is `0`.

- max_p:

  Numeric in \[0, 1\]. Edges with p-value strictly above this value are
  removed. Default is `1`.

- remove_isolates:

  Logical. If `TRUE`, vertices with degree 0 after pruning are removed.
  Default is `FALSE`.

## Value

A pruned `catmodgraph` object.

## Examples

``` r
df <- expand_table(Titanic)
mg <- build_modality_graph(df)
mg2 <- prune_modality_edges(mg, min_weight = 0.1, max_p = 0.05)
mg2
#> $graph
#> IGRAPH 7ddabf6 UNW- 10 26 -- 
#> + attr: name (v/c), variable (v/c), modality (v/c), weight (e/n),
```
